It is closely regulated by the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) as rising cases of cancer and heart diseases due to cigarette smoking is a serious concern. Smoking causes more than 480,000 deaths annually in the United States.</p><p>Amid this scenario, governments around the world have been imposing stringent restrictions on tobacco companies to lower cigarette consumption. Such restrictions have severely dented businesses of tobacco majors including Philip Morris International Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/PM">PM</a>, Altria Group Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/MO">MO</a>, British American Tobacco p.l.c. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/BTI">BTI</a> and Vector Group Ltd. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/VGR">VGR</a>.</p><p>In a recent move, Winston-Salem-based Reynolds American, which is being acquired by British American, along with Richmond, Va-based Altria and other cigarette makers is set to put up self-critical advertisements on television and newspapers to dissuade customers from smoking per court orders.</p><p>Apart from this, the court wants tobacco companies to admit that cigarettes have been intentionally made addictive through the issuance of corrective ads starting Nov 26. Per the <em>Wall Street Journal</em>, the move comes in the wake of settling a 1999 lawsuit which accused the industry for several health hazards.</p><p>Notably since 2009, the FDA has been imposing restrictions on cigarette companies over selling and packaging. In July, the FDA urged tobacco makers to lower nicotine levels in cigarettes, as tar and other substances inhaled through smoking is detrimental to health.</p><p>Not only this, the FDA has made it mandatory for tobacco companies to use precautionary labels on cigarette packets to dissuade customers from smoking. The European Union and the FDA have proposed a ban on menthol in accordance with the Tobacco Control Act. Per the act, menthol has an adverse effect on health and thus should not be used in any product.</p><p>Recently, the state government in India\'s capital directed Philip Morris and other tobacco companies to remove all advertisements in the city, warning them of legal action if they do not comply.</p><p><strong>Switch to Cigarette Alternatives</strong></p><p>Amid increasing government restrictions and declining smoking rates, tobacco giants have introduced e-cigarettes and switched to less harmful &lsquo;Reduced Risk Products&rsquo; to boost their business and mitigate loss. However, the FDA has imposed several restrictions on e-cigarettes as well.</p><p>The FDA made it mandatory for all tobacco makers to seek marketing authorization for any tobacco product introduced after Feb 15, 2007. The law was extended to include e-cigarettes, pipe tobacco, cigars and hookah. The FDA has currently deferred its reviews for products like cigars and hookah tobacco until 2021 and e-cigarettes until 2022.</p><p><strong>Share Price Performance: Industry Versus S&amp;P 500</strong></p><p>Given the aforementioned turmoil, it is not at all surprising that the <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/industry/tobaco-183">Zacks Tobacco industry</a> is currently placed at the bottom 28% out of the 265 Zacks Classified Industries. The industry has slumped 7.5% in the last six months, against the S&amp;P 500 market&rsquo;s 8.4% growth.</p><p><strong><img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/zadmin_tuner_image/tobacco_2017_10_06.jpg" style="width: 620px; height: 195px;" /></strong></p><p><strong>Bottom Line</strong></p><p>Stricter regulations have adversely impacted tobacco makers&rsquo; revenues. The market is getting crowded and seeing increased pricing pressure.', 'content': [{'base': u'http://feed.zacks.com/commentary/AllStories/rss', 'type': u'text/html', 'value': u'<p>Hepatitis C is an infectious disease caused by the hepatitis C virus (HCV) that primarily affects the liver. Gilead Sciences Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/GILD">GILD</a> markets blockbuster HCV drugs, Sovaldi and Harvoni, while other well-known names in this market are AbbVie Inc.&rsquo;s <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/ABBV">ABBV</a> Viekira Pak, Bristol-Myers&rsquo; <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/BMY">BMY</a> Daklinza and Johnson &amp; Johnson&rsquo;s <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/JNJ">JNJ</a> Olysio.</p><p>According to the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC), about 3.2 million people in the United States are living with chronic hepatitis C infection while many remain unaware of being infected. There are about 17,000 new hepatitis C cases each year in the United States, many of which go unreported.<br /><br />Considering these numbers, it is not a surprise that quite a few pharma and biotech companies are working on bringing new, improved, shorter-duration HCV treatments to the market. The market is thus getting crowded and seeing increased pricing pressure. &nbsp;</p><p>A lot has happened in the HCV space of late. &nbsp;</p><p>In September 2017, Gilead Sciences&rsquo; Sovaldi received approval in China, as a component of a combination antiviral treatment regimen. It is the first Gilead HCV drug to be approved in China. &nbsp;</p><p>Meanwhile, Gilead&rsquo;s single-tablet regimen (STR) of Sovaldi, velpatasvir and voxilaprevir, Vosevi received approval in the United States, EU and Canada in July/August. Vosevi became the first once-daily STR available as a salvage therapy for patients infected with HCV genotype 1&ndash;6 who have failed prior treatment with DAA regimens including NS5A inhibitors.</p><p>Gilead&rsquo;s shares have outperformed the industry year to date. The stock has rallied 16.6% compared with the <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/industry/medical-biomedical-and-genetics-105">industry&rsquo;</a>s gain of 14.5% in the same time frame. The stock carries a Zacks Rank #3 (Hold). You can see<strong> <a href="https://www.zacks.com/registration/premium/login/?continue_to=%2Fstocks%2Fbuy-list%2F%3FADID%3Dzp_1link%26ICID%3Dzpi_1link">the complete list of today&rsquo;s Zacks #1 Rank (Strong Buy) stocks here</a>.</strong></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong><img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/zadmin_tuner_image/gild_2017_10_06.jpg" style="width: 620px; height: 194px;" /></strong></p><p>Meanwhile, AbbVie&rsquo;s 8-week, pan-genotypic, ribavirin-free, once-daily HCV treatment, Mavyret/Maviret, gained approval in the United States, EU and Canada in the past couple of months. Mavyret, AbbVie&rsquo;s next-generation HCV program, is a combination of glecaprevir, a potent protease inhibitor and pibrentasvir, a NS5A inhibitor. Maviret has the potential to rejuvenate growth in the HCV franchise. According to AbbVie, Mavyret may be used in up to 95% of HCV patients, depending on the stage of liver disease and prior treatment history.</p><p>Abbvie&rsquo;s shares have outperformed the industry year to date. The stock has rallied 44% compared with the <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/industry/large-cap-pharmaceuticals-225">industry</a>&rsquo;s gain of 17.9% in the same time frame. The stock carries a Zacks Rank #3.</p><p><img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/zadmin_tuner_image/abbv_2017_10_06.jpg" style="width: 620px; height: 199px;" /></p><p>However, last week, pharmaceutical giant Merck <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/MRK">MRK</a> announced that it is discontinuing further development of two of its next-generation hepatitis C (HCV) programs &mdash; MK-3682B (grazoprevir/ruzasvir/ uprifosbuvir) and MK-3682C (ruzasvir/uprifosbuvir). The company made this decision based on review of available phase II efficacy data and a heavily crowded HCV market.</p><p>Merck&rsquo;s shares have underperformed the industry year to date. The stock has gained 9.7% compared with the <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/industry/large-cap-pharmaceuticals-225">industry</a>&rsquo;s gain of 17.9% in the same time frame. The stock carries a Zacks Rank #3.</p><p><img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/zadmin_tuner_image/mrk_2017_10_06.jpg" style="width: 620px; height: 195px;" /></p><p>Besides Merck, another giant Johnson &amp; Johnson also discontinued the development of its investigational HCV treatment regimen JNJ-4178, a combination of three direct acting antivirals: AL-335, odalasvir and simeprevir. Litigation issues related to past misconducts continue for banks. Recently, at a heated Senate meeting, <strong>Wells Fargo &amp; Company</strong>&rsquo;s <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/WFC">WFC</a> CEO Timothy Sloan vigorously tried to defend America&rsquo;s third-largest bank for its past wrongdoings amid a volley of questions raised by senators.</p><p>Sloan was grilled for forcing the affected customers of fake accounts scandal into arbitration, in his bid to avoid courtroom hassles. He responded saying that the bank did not prevent its customers from suing and would not do so in the future either. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277695/wells-fargo-ceo-faces-us-senators-fury-over-scandals">Wells Fargo CEO Faces U.S. Senators\' Fury Over Scandals</a>)<br /><br />Amid mounting litigation issues, the Office of the Comptroller of the Currency (OCC) might charge Wells Fargo with new penalties for issues related to car insurance and mortgage loans. The bank is under OCC&rsquo;s investigation for improperly charging customers for car insurance and mortgage loans, reported this year.</p><p>Therefore, if the inquiry reveals a violation of the agreement, known as a &lsquo;Matter Requiring Attention&rsquo; to finish off unfair and deceptive business malpractices, the bank will be charged with new penalties. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277536/wells-fargo-wfc-might-cringe-with-new-regulatory-penalties">Wells Fargo Might Cringe With New Regulatory Penalties</a>)<br /><br />2. <strong>Citigroup Inc.</strong> <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/C">C</a>, has agreed to pay $550,000 to the Commodity Futures Trading Commission (CFTC), as penalty for violations in reporting swap transaction and absence of proper reporting procedure since April 2015 to December 2016. Citibank and London-based Citigroup Global Markets, two subsidiaries of Citigroup, have been charged for improper reporting of Legal Entity Identifier data for swap transactions.</p><p>Citi has also been accused of failing to remove errors in such data. However, the commission added that the company cooperated well during the investigation. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277174/citigroup-to-pay-penalty-for-violations-in-swap-reporting">Citigroup to Pay Penalty for Violations in Swap Reporting</a>)<br /><br />In another case, Citigroup has agreed to pay $1.74 billion to the estate of Lehman Brothers Holdings Inc. for a case that was filed during the 2008 financial crisis. The settlement comes as a tailwind for Lehman&rsquo;s unsecured creditors in the 10-year old bankruptcy case.</p><p>Citigroup had claimed that Lehman owed it $2 billion as a result of bankruptcy. Lehman accused Citigroup of making a false claim, as at that time it had access to $2.1 billion it had on deposit for trades with the bank. Lehman also charged the company of making up extra costs and using unfair methods in order to justify its claim. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277421/citigroup-to-settle-10year-old-dispute-with-lehman-brothers">Citigroup to Settle 10-Year Old Dispute With Lehman Brothers</a>)<br /><br />3. <strong>KeyCorp</strong> <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/KEY">KEY</a>, through its corporate and investment banking unit, KeyBanc Capital Markets Inc., has completed the acquisition of Cain Brothers &amp; Company, LLC. The deal, announced on Aug 15, 2017, was aimed at expanding the company&rsquo;s existing healthcare investment banking. The move seems to be a good expansion strategy for KeyCorp as healthcare is one of the largest sectors in the United States and there is a growing need for distinctive capabilities.</p><p>Moreover, with this buyout, KeyCorp seems to be on track to become a leading corporate and investment bank. The deal should supplement KeyCorp\'s capabilities and leverage its network. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277769/keycorp-closes-cain-brothers-deal-expands-health-advisory">KeyCorp Closes Cain Brothers\' Deal, Expands Health Advisory</a>)<br /><br />4. In order to shift operations post Brexit, Citigroup is applying for a French broker license, per James Cowles, chief executive officer for Europe, the Middle East &amp; Africa. Previously, on Britain&rsquo;s exit, the company had declared Frankfurt as headquarter for trading operations in the European Union. It also announced plans to develop investment and private banking operations in the region.</p><p>Cowles said that Brexit would impact about 100-200 jobs. The positions would be transferred between one of its seven core locations across Europe, including Frankfurt, Paris, Milan and Luxembourg. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277405/citigroup-applies-for-broker-license-in-france-post-brexit">Citigroup Applies for Broker License in France Post Brexit</a>)<br /><br />5. In order to improve operating efficiencies, <strong>BB&amp;T Corporation</strong> <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/BBT">BBT</a> is shutting down its call center at the former Susquehanna Bank headquarters in Lititz, PA. As a result, of its roughly 125 employees, 82 will lose their jobs. The remaining employees will be relocated to the bank&rsquo;s other facilities in the county. The call center basically catered to BB&amp;T&rsquo;s back office operations, including administrative and support. The staff members did not deal directly with customers. They will have to leave by mid-December. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277841/bbampt-bbt-to-close-pennsylvania-call-center-amp-cut-82-jobs">BB&amp;T to Close Pennsylvania Call Center &amp; Cut 82 Jobs</a>)<br /><br />6. <strong>Bank of the Ozarks</strong> <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/OZRK">OZRK</a> announced a 2.8% hike in its quarterly cash dividend. The new dividend of 18.5 cents per share will be paid on Oct 20 to shareholders on record as of Oct 13. This is the 29th consecutive quarterly increase in dividend by the bank. Given a solid capital and liquidity position, the company is expected to continue enhancing shareholder value through efficient capital deployment activities. (Read more: <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277616/is-bank-of-the-ozarks-stock-worth-a-look-post-dividend-hike">Is Bank of the Ozarks Stock Worth a Look Post Dividend Hike?</a>)<br /><br /><strong>Price Performance</strong><br /><br />Here is how the seven major stocks performed:<br />&nbsp;</p><table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 238px;" width="238"><tbody><tr><td nowrap="nowrap" style="width: 72px; u'<p>The future of the U.S. healthcare space is mired in uncertainty with President Trump&rsquo;s efforts to revoke the Affordable Care Act (ACA) or Obamacare falling flat. This is despite the fact that the Republicans are going all out to end the policy fiasco. The investment world is equally baffled.</p><p><strong>Chances of Stability Anytime Soon?</strong></p><p>The majority of the healthcare space has heaved a sigh of relief with the recent failure of the Graham-Cassidy bill, thanks to the Congressional Budget Office&rsquo;s (CBO) latest &lsquo;warning report&rsquo; that anticipated health coverage loss for millions of Americans due to $1 trillion in reduction in federal spending on Medicaid through 2026.</p><p>Per the report, there will be considerable decrease in the number of people enrolling in Medicaid in this period for three primary reasons &mdash; &ldquo;the expansion of the program established by the ACA would be repealed starting in 2020, federal reimbursement to states for Medicaid would be capped on a per-en-rollee basis beginning in 2020, and the individual mandate penalty (which induces some people to enroll in Medicaid) would be repealed upon the legislation&rsquo;s enactment.&rdquo;</p><p>Although the President&rsquo;s latest action plan indicates that the respite from Graham-Cassidy failure is short-lived, one thing is pretty clear from the entire pandemonium. Any effort to bring about a major change in the existing health insurance policy may again turn out to be futile for the Republicans.</p><p>This is because, in their undying effort to fully repeal and replace Obamacare, the Republicans have never achieved a 60-40 majority. Among the related articles doing the rounds, a report by Kimberly Amadeo published in The Balance states that &ldquo;Trump wanted Congress to replace the Affordable Care Act of 2010 before September 30, 2017. That\'s the last day Senate Republicans could pass the bill with just a 51-vote majority. That includes Vice President Mike Pence casting the final vote. But they never got the votes.&rdquo;</p><p>While economists are once again dissecting all the facts trying to come out with probable ways in which the ruling party can turn around, it is hard for investors keen on the medical space to settle for an investment strategy that can earn them a concrete pay.</p><p><strong>Investing Strategy to Bet On</strong></p><p>Amid such political conundrum, while pondering on several investment mantras, the majority of investors prefer to bet on stocks, which have ability to brave the situation with their rock-solid fundamentals. brought much needed stability to the market with prices set to improve steadily. Multinational oil enterprises (like Chevron), on the back of greater certainty, will now be able revive spending on drilling activities. In fact, being one of the most oil-weighted majors, Chevron is likely to outperform its peers in case of the commodity\'s rebound as per our expectations.</p><p><strong>Strong Pipeline:</strong> Chevron&rsquo;s existing oil and gas development project pipeline is among the best in the industry &ndash; targeting volume growth of 4-9% in 2017 &ndash; driven by the big Australian LNG projects (Gorgon and Wheatstone), as well as deepwater developments in the U.S. Gulf of Mexico and the Permian operations. In particular, with increasing amounts of capital spending devoted to the lucrative unconventional play over the coming years, production from the Permian region is expected to be strong.</p><p><strong>Estimates Moving Up: </strong>Annual estimates for Chevron have moved north in the past 30 days, reflecting analysts&rsquo; confidence on the stock. In this period, the Zacks Consensus Estimate for 2017 has increased by around 2% to $4.02 per share. The Zacks Consensus Estimate for 2018 has also moved up 1.5% to $4.59.</p><p><strong>Sound Q2 Performance: </strong>Chevron reported adjusted earnings per share of 91 cents in the second-quarter, up 90% from 48 cents per share in the prior-year quarter and higher than the Zacks Consensus Estimate of 89 cents.</p><p><strong>Positive Earnings Surprise History: </strong>Chevron has outpaced the Zacks Consensus Estimate in three of the trailing four quarters, delivering a positive average earnings surprise of 19.4%.</p><p><strong>Prudent Expenses Management:</strong> As a result of Chevron\'s focus on well planning and execution, the company continues to reduce its operating costs with underlying expenses down almost 10% year-to-date compared to 2016. Capital expenditures for the first six months of the year are also down 25%.</p><p><strong>Asset Sale on Track:</strong> The recent divestment of downstream assets in Canada to fuel distributor Parkland is part of Chevron\'s strategy to exit noncompetitive projects, while lowering cost and capital expenditure. Apart from a leaner business model, it will also help Chevron to progress toward its $5-$10 billion divestment goals during 2016-2017.</p><p><strong>Healthy Growth Prospects: </strong>The Zacks Consensus Estimate for revenues is at $133.3 billion for 2017, reflecting 16.4% year-over-year growth. The estimate for 2018 of $140.5 billion projects 5.4% annual growth. The Zacks Consensus Estimate for earnings for 2017 is pegged at $4.02, depicting growth of 302.4%. The estimate for 2018 reflects year-over-year growth of 14.2%.</p><p>The stock has an estimated long-term earnings growth rate of 23.9%, higher than the industry average of 7.9%.</p><p>Despite these key driving factors, we advise investors to wait for a better entry point before buying shares in the oil major. The trend is expected to continue for the next few quarters, with the company relying on asset sales and debt to plug the deficit.</p><p><strong>Dependence on Few Large Projects: </strong>Chevron targets to grow volume by 4-9% in 2017. In particular, Chevron\'s high-profile Gorgon LNG development in Australia is suffering from mechanical issues that may restrict its ramp-up.</p><p><strong>Nigeria Exposure:</strong> Chevron\'s exposure to production in the vulnerable and violence-prone regions in Nigeria poses additional risk.</p><p><strong>Stocks to Consider</strong></p><p>Better-ranked stocks in the energy space include Lonestar Resources US Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/LONE">LONE</a> and Transocean Ltd. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/RIG">RIG</a>. Lonestar sports a Zacks Rank #1 (Strong Buy), while Transocean carries a Zacks Rank #2 (Buy). United States, President Donald Trump proposed changes in tax rates for both individuals and corporates.</p><p>At present, the U.S. corporations have to pay up to 35%, one of the highest in the world, on repatriated foreign incomes. However, it gives tax credit for the amount of tax paid in overseas country.</p><p>The tax holiday plan proposes to lower the current corporate tax rate of 35% to 15%. This is expected to favorably impact the post-tax earnings of companies. The Trump administration is also proposing a move away from the current worldwide tax system to a territorial system, allowing companies to send offshore profits back to the United Stateswithout incurring extra taxes.</p><p>Another major reform proposed is the repatriation of trillions of dollars held as cash reserve overseas by the companies with global operations for one-time tax (reportedly 10%).</p><div class="chart_embed"><p><strong>Computer and Technology Sector 5YR % Return</strong></p><p><a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/sector/computer-and-technology-4"> <img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/charts/2f/1507289965.png" title="" /> </a></p><p><a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/sector/computer-and-technology-4">Computer and Technology Sector 5YR % Return</a></p></div><p><strong>Impact of the Proposal</strong></p><p>In 2004, the Bush administration attempted a similar repatriation tax holiday for bringing in overseas cash reserves for one-time tax of 5.25%. A number of companies repatriated an amount exceeding $300 billion.</p><p>The tax reforms are anticipated to create new jobs and aid economic growth through expanded investment as more cash will be available to companies. Consequently, a revision of tax rate to 15% will not bring a huge positive change in post-tax earnings. Hence, Alphabet is anticipated to be positively impacted by these reforms, through stock repurchases and dividends payout.</p><p>Alphabet currently carries a Zacks Rank #3 and has a long-term expected EPS growth rate 16.5%.</p><p><strong>Bottom Line</strong></p><p>The tax reform isn\'t going to be easy and is still in the proposal period. The global steel industry continues to reel under the effects of excess capacity &ndash; the biggest obstacle to persistent growth and profitability.&nbsp; &nbsp;<br /><br />Meanwhile, U.S. steel mills remain impacted by low capacity utilization and a more pressing problem &ndash; renewed flood of cheap imports. A surge in steel imports have put downward pressure on U.S. steel prices during the third quarter.<br /><br /><strong>Steel Demand Poised for Steady Recovery</strong><br /><br />The steel industry is poised to benefit from solid demand in the United States and emerging markets this year. The World Steel Association (WSA) &ndash; the international trade body for the iron and steel industry &ndash; expects global steel demand to expand 1.3% in 2017 following a 1% rise in 2016.</p><p>A cyclical upturn in steel demand is expected to be supported by an ongoing recovery in the developed economies along with an accelerating growth momentum in the emerging and developing economies.<br /><br />The United States is expected to lead growth in the developed world thanks to strong fundamentals, measures related to fiscal stimuli and rising infrastructure spending. Steel demand in the United States is expected to rise 3% this year.<br /><br />Demand in emerging and developing economies (barring China) is also expected to rise 4% this year.</p><p><strong>Too Much Steel Poses a Concern</strong><br /><br />The global steel industry continues bear the brunt of a surge in production in China &ndash; the world\'s biggest steel maker. According to WSA, global crude steel production went up 4.9% year over year during the first eight months of 2017.<br /><br />Output from China, which accounts for around half of the global production, climbed 5.6% year over year during the first eight months of the year. Production from the country also shot up 8.7% year over year to a monthly record of 74.6 Mt in August.<br /><br />China&rsquo;s steel juggernaut continues to gather steam notwithstanding the global production glut. Steel mills in the country are ramping up production to take advantage of a spike in domestic steel prices that translates to higher profits for the industry.<br /><br />Nevertheless, production cuts are expected later this year as Beijing pushes forward with supply-side structural reform to streamline its burgeoning steel sector. China, earlier this year, announced plans to cut its steel production capacity by around 50 million metric tons in 2017 in a bid to reduce overcapacity and control pollution.<br /><br /><strong>Imports Still Haunting U.S. Mills</strong><br /><br />The American market continues to be inundated with cheap steel imports from overseas producers despite a raft of punitive trade actions. According to a recent report from the American Iron and Steel Institute (AISI), total and finished steel imports for the first eight months of 2017 shot up 20.6% and 15.5% year over year, respectively. Year to date, finished steel import market share is estimated at 28%, which is higher than 26% clocked in full-year 2016.<br /><br />While positive rulings in trade cases (resulting in levy of heavy tariffs) against China last year led to a decline in Chinese steel exports to the United States, imports from other countries remain at above historical levels.<br /><br />U.S. steel producers, Nucor Corp. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/NUE">NUE</a> and Steel Dynamics, Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/STLD">STLD</a> recently provided lower-than-expected earnings guidance for the third quarter saying that high levels of steel imports have put pressure on domestic steel prices during the quarter.<br /><br />Continued import pressure has not allowed steel pricing to keep pace with higher raw material costs during the third quarter. U.S. hot-rolled coil steel prices retreated in September and some analysts expect prices to weaken through the balance of the year. High import levels are likely to keep U.S. steel prices in check.<br /><br /><strong>Can Section 232 Bring Relief?</strong><br /><br />U.S. steel makers are pinning their hopes on President Trump imposing new restrictions on imported steel. Steel stocks got a shot in the arm in April 2017 after the Trump administration ordered an investigation under Section 232 of the Trade Expansion Act of 1962. The Section 232 probe is aimed at determining whether the imports pose a threat to national security and also gives the President the power to impose broad tariffs or quotas on imported steel.<br /><br />However, the Trump administration has delayed the release of the report on the Section 232 probe, which was initially expected at the end of June 2017. U.S. Commerce Secretary Wilbur Ross in an interview told Bloomberg last month that a decision on steel tariffs has been delayed until after the completion of the tax reform. The U.S. Department of Commerce has until mid-January 2018 to conclude the investigation.<br /><br />A delay in the Section 232 probe has triggered a spike in steel imports into the American market in the recent months. While the findings from the Section 232 steel investigation are due, a positive outcome from the probe will give the Trump administration the opportunity to take broad-based trade actions against cheap imports. u'http://feed.zacks.com/commentary/AllStories/rss', 'type': u'text/html', 'value': u'<p>Even though it is true that airline stocks are being confronted with multiple headwinds, all is not lost. There exist a few bright spots that still make investment in airline stocks worthwhile. Let&rsquo;s delve into the details.</p><p><strong>Oil Still Below $55 = Financial Prosperity</strong></p><p>Despite the recent rally, oil prices are still hovering around the $50-a-barrel mark, a long way off the highs of mid-2014 when the commodity had traded in excess of $100 a barrel. As fuel costs represent one of the largest input costs for airline companies, the lower the oil prices, the better it is for sector participants. Lower oil prices imply greater financial well-being for airlines by virtue of massive savings.</p><p>Financial prosperity is reflected in the fact that the likes of Southwest Airlines (<acronym class="ticker">LUV</acronym>), Delta Air Lines (<acronym class="ticker">DAL</acronym>) and Alaska Air Group (<acronym class="ticker">ALK</acronym>) have hiked their respective dividend payouts this year. Carriers have also indulged in share buybacks, which is more proof of their solid financial health.</p><p>Riding on balance sheet strength, some carriers have shelled out impressive amounts to employees as part of their profit-sharing programs. Additionally, the robust financial health of most domestic carriers has prompted them to invest substantially in improving the flying experience for travelers, in a bid to stay afloat in the competitive airline space. For example, United Airlines, the wholly owned subsidiary of United Continental Holdings (<acronym class="ticker">UAL</acronym>), announced in July, the introduction of Boeing 777-300ER service (the airline&rsquo;s latest aircraft type featuring the all-new United Polaris business class seats) to additional routes.</p><p>Carriers are also investing substantially toward modernizing their respective fleet. For example, American Airlines Group (<acronym class="ticker">AAL</acronym>) invested $1.1 billion in a new aircraft during the second quarter of 2017. In fact, it aims to shell out $4.1 billion in the current year for the same purpose. Moreover, carriers like Delta and JetBlue Airways (<acronym class="ticker">JBLU</acronym>) are looking to reduce their debt levels based on their financial prosperity.</p><p><strong>Bullish Readings</strong></p><p>The global traffic data for July, released by the International Air Transport Association (&ldquo;IATA&rdquo;) raises optimism. Load factor (percentage of seats filled by passengers) touched record levels of 84.7% in July. The upside was due to the fact that traffic growth (6.8%) outpaced capacity expansion (6.1%) for the month. The favorable load factor reading highlights the fact that demand for air travel is strong.</p><p>Moreover, demand for air freight across the globe witnessed double-digit growth (11.4%) in July. This was, in fact, the fourth month out of five where double-digit demand growth was witnessed. The reading is well above the 10-year average growth rate of 3.1%. With growth in demand outpacing capacity expansion, the scenario bodes well for airline yields.</p><p>Traffic growth witnessed by the industry in the first half of 2017 was the highest in 12 years. Load factor also touched record levels. Additionally, at its 73<sup>rd</sup> Annual General Meeting in Cancun, Mexico, IATA stated that airline companies are expected to be more profitable in 2017 than previously expected. IATA now expects global net profit for the industry to come in at $31.4 billion (the earlier projection hinted at profits of $29.8 billion for 2017). The bulk of global profits ($15.4 billion) is expected to come from the North American region.</p><p>Traffic data for the first half of 2017 released by the U.S. Department of Transportation&rsquo;s Bureau of Transportation Statistics (BTS) also highlights the bullish case for carriers based in the United States. The BTS data states that a record number of passengers were transported by U.S.-based carriers in the period. The reading for load factor was also favorable.</p><p>Moreover, the busy Labor Day travel period (Aug 30-Sep 5) for U.S. airlines this year further highlights that demand for air travel remains strong. This bodes well for airlines.</p><p><strong>Other Tailwinds</strong></p><p>High labor costs have been hurting bottom-line growth for airlines for quite some time. Even though such costs will remain a hindrance, the good news is that the extent of their increase is expected to decline with time.</p><p>For example, American Airlines predicted in September that cost per available seat miles(excluding fuel and special Items) the year-over-year growth is likely to be around 3% in the final quarter of 2017. The metric had grown by 7.6% and 6.8%, respectively, in the first two quarters of 2017. The year-over-year growth for this measure of unit costs is likely to come down further to less than 2% in 2018/19.</p><p>Latin American carriers like GOL Linhas (<acronym class="ticker">GOL</acronym>) are seeing better times, buoyed by an improved economy. GOL&rsquo;s view for full-year 2017 is impressive. We expect the company&rsquo;s focus on capacity discipline to result in improvement in yields, going forward. GOL Linhas holds a Zacks Rank #2 (Buy). You can see&nbsp;<a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/buy-list/?ADID=zp_1link&amp;ICID=zpi%20_1link" title="blocked::https://www.zacks.com/stocks/buy-list/?ADID=zp_1link&amp;ICID=zpi _1link"><strong>the complete list of today&rsquo;s Zacks #1 Rank (Strong Buy) stocks here</strong></a>.</p><p>European low-cost carrier <strong>Ryanair Holdings</strong> (<acronym class="ticker">RYAAY</acronym>), which is being aided by its customer-friendly &lsquo;Always Getting Better&rsquo; campaign, unveiled a busy London schedule for the summer of 2018, amid Brexit-related fears. The carrier aims to transport 24.8 million customers from three London airports &mdash; Stansted, Gatwick and Luton. With the Greek economy showing signs of revival, exciting times might be in store for Ryanair as it offers multiple flights to the Greek Islands.</p><p><strong>To Wrap Up</strong></p><p>The above commentary clearly suggests that despite headwinds, there exist enough reasons to be bullish about the industry&rsquo;s prospects. But scientists in university labs and at biotechnology companies big and small have been hard at work on cracking the chemical codes of communication between human T-cells, the body\'s disease warriors, and cancer cells.</p><p>One of these &quot;immuno-therapies&quot; is called CAR-T, a technology which uses <em>chimeric antigen receptors</em> to activate T-cells. And one company I\'ve followed for a while in this space, where we just locked in 70% gains in my Healthcare Innovators portfolio, is Juno Therapeutics (JUNO). Here\'s how they describe their science...</p><p><em>Juno is focused on revolutionizing medicine by re-engaging the body\'s immune system to treat cancer. Founded on the vision that the use of human T cells as therapeutics will drive one of the next important phases in medicine, we are developing cell-based cancer immunotherapies based on our chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) and high-affinity T cell receptor (TCR) technologies to genetically engineer T cells to recognize and kill cancer cells. We have shown compelling evidence of tumor shrinkage in clinical trials using multiple cell-based product candidates to address refractory B-cell lymphomas and leukemias. Longer term, Juno aims to develop our cell-based platform to include additional product candidates to address a broad range of cancers and human diseases.</em></p><p>Why is this such a huge discovery? The answer is probably obvious if you or anyone you know has had cancer and gone through surgery, radiation treatment, or chemotherapy. Those &quot;cures&quot; are painful, risky, and don\'t always work.</p><p>To genetically engineer a patient\'s own T cells to recognize and attack cancer is a revolutionary and most welcome breakthrough in oncology treatment.</p><p>While this science is still in its early stages, the clinical results have been inspiring and gaining FDA &quot;fast-track&quot; designation to speed the R&amp;D process. Throughout the chip-making market, companies have successfully adapted to the changing needs of the consumer, including an increased demand for small, high-powered chips that enable &ldquo;Internet of Things&rdquo; (IoT) devices.</p><p>For those that don&rsquo;t know, the Internet of Things is the growing world of interconnected household and industrial devices. Everyday products and machines can now be embedded with sensor technology to process data or interact with other electronic devices.</p><p>For example, consumer-level IoT products include things like Amazon&rsquo;s (AMZN) Echo &ldquo;smart speaker,&rdquo; wearable motion and activity tracking products, and advanced in-car technology. On the commercial side of the IoT market, industrial manufacturers have begun implementing sensors into machines to track performance and efficiency.</p><p><strong>(Also Read: </strong><a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/231964/how-to-invest-in-the-internet-of-things"><strong>How to Invest in the &quot;Internet of Things&quot;</strong></a><strong>) </strong></p><p>As demand for the microchips that power these IoT devices continues to grow, semiconductor manufacturers with a focus on IoT products will continue to benefit. With that said, we&rsquo;ve found three already-strong stocks that are looking to benefit even more from further IoT growth.</p><p><strong>1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </strong><strong>Texas Instruments (</strong><a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/TXN">TXN</a><strong>)</strong></p><p>Although you might recognize the brand because of its calculators, Texas Instruments is actually one of the leading suppliers of advanced semiconductors in the world. The company&rsquo;s IoT profile falls under its Embedded Processors division, which includes the Connectivity, Microcontrollers, and Processors categories. In its most recent earnings report, Texas Instruments saw growth of 15% in its Embedded Processors segment, and that&rsquo;s not to mention that it once again surpassed our consensus estimates for earnings and revenue. Texas Instruments is currently a Zacks Rank #2 (Buy), and on top of this, the company pays a nice 2.44% dividend.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </strong><strong>ON Semiconductor (</strong><a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/ON">ON</a><strong>)</strong></p><p>ON Semiconductor has traditionally been known as a power management and commodity chip maker, but the company has started to carve out a budding IoT division. ON is now heavily involved with automotive solutions, and its IoT offerings also include products catered to wearables, smart city development, and industrial automation. Currently, the stock is sporting a Zacks Rank #1 (Strong Buy) and an overall VGM grade of &ldquo;A.&rdquo; ON has emerged as an exciting growth pick, with current consensus estimates calling for EPS growth of 75% and sales growth of 38% this fiscal year. The company&rsquo;s P/E ratio of 13.75 and P/S ratio of 1.61 also work to show that its shares may be undervalued right now.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </strong><strong>Vishay Intertechnology (</strong><a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/VSH">VSH</a><strong>)</strong></p><p>Vishay Intertechnology is a global manufacturer and supplier of discrete semiconductors. The company has a broad portfolio of unique passive and active solutions that are tailored to the &ldquo;things&rdquo; being controlled in the IoT. Vishay markets its portfolio to manufacturers of everything from biometric monitoring systems to fitbands and smart appliances. The stock is currently a Zacks Rank #1 (Strong Buy) and has an &ldquo;A&rdquo; grade for Value. VSH has a P/E ratio of 14.51, as well as a PEG ratio of 0.71 and a P/S ratio of 1.18&mdash;all figures that suggest its shares are undervalued. Also, based on our current consensus estimates, we expect to see Vishay post EPS growth of 58% and sales growth of 9% this fiscal year.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Bottom Line</strong></p><p>The Internet of Things is one of the most exciting emerging tech markets in the world. Home automation products are fun. In-car technology is cool.</p><p>And while these specific products are interesting, the real moneymakers in these situations are the companies that are building the tech that powers these products. The Internet of Things needs semiconductors to function, and as the IoT grows, so too will semiconductor companies.</p><p>The best way for investors to cash in on this growing trend is to identify semiconductor companies that are not only investing in the Internet of Things, but are also displaying solid fundamentals and impressive Zacks metrics.</p><p><em>Want more stock market analysis from this author? <b>Encana Corporation</b> <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/ECA">ECA</a> has recently announced operating two of its three Veresen Midstream facilities well ahead of the scheduled time and that too within budget. These production sites are supposed to support Encana&rsquo;s condensate-focused growth plan, representing the Montney formation located in British Columbia. Notably, Calgary, Canada-based Veresen Midstream has inked an innovative midstream agreement with Encana, helping the latter to build and operate the three plants.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">While the Tower and Sunrise facilities in Montney formation came online in September-end, Encana expects the Saturn facility, which is also ahead of schedule, to start before the end of 2017. The plants are supposed to increase the company&rsquo;s Montney liquids production by more than double its fourth-quarter 2016 level. Per a fee-for-service agreement, Encana pays to use the three Veresen Midstream-owned facilities.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Also, the Towerbirch lateral pipeline, which will aid Encana&rsquo;s operations in Montney, started functioning from the beginning of this October. The pipeline connects the Tower, Sunrise and Saturn facilities with the NOVA Gas Transmission Ltd. (&ldquo;NGTL&rdquo;) system.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Delivering complex projects like those under budget limits and prior to their scheduled dates, shows the company&rsquo;s competence level. This efficiency will further add stimulus to cement the bond between Encana and Veresen Midstream, thereby opening future building-contract opportunities for the former on behalf of the latter.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Despite Encana&rsquo;s production being constrained at an average of 3,500 barrels of oil equivalent per day (BOE/d) in third-quarter 2017 due to Hurricane Harvey&rsquo;s catastrophic effects in Texan region, the company expects to achieve its current-year production guidance on the back of pre-scheduled startups in Montney.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>About Encana</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Based in Calgary, Alberta, Encana is a focused pure-play natural gas exploration and production (E&amp;P) company. It is the second largest gas producer in North America, holding a highly competitive land and resource position among a number of most promising shale and tight gas resource plays in the region. This provides the company with a low risk, long-life and a sustainable growth profile.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Encana&rsquo;s cost-reduction initiative and divestment of high-cost low-profit assets offer financial flexibility to the company to handle the current volatile market condition in a better fashion. However, the company&rsquo;s huge exposure to natural gas remains a key area of concern with the commodity price still languishing below the key psychological level of $3 per million British Thermal Units.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>Price performance</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Encana has lost 2.4% of its value year to date, underperforming the 1.2% fall of its <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/industry/oil-and-gas-exploration-and-production-canadian-129">industry</a>.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/zadmin_tuner_image/ecakpd.jpg" /></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>Zacks Rank and Stocks to Consider</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Encana currently carries a Zacks Rank #3 (Hold).</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Some better-ranked stocks in the oil and energy sector are Lonestar Resources US Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/LONE">LONE</a>, Alliance Holdings GP, L.P. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/AHGP">AHGP</a> and First Solar, Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/FSLR">FSLR</a>, all sporting a Zacks Rank #1 (Strong Buy). Let's discuss whether GoPro's products can withstand the competition and retain its market share.", 'language': None}, 'published_parsed': time.struct_time(tm_year=2017, tm_mon=10, tm_mday=6, tm_hour=16, tm_min=31, tm_sec=0, tm_wday=4, tm_yday=279, tm_isdst=0), 'links': [{'href': u'http://www.zacks.com/stock/news/278028/can-gopros-fusion-360-and-hero-6-fend-off-competition?cid=CS-ZC-FT-278028', 'type': u'text/html', 'rel': u'alternate'}], 'title': u"Can GoPro's Fusion 360 and Hero 6 Fend Off Competition?", 'authors': [{'name': u'Zacks Equity Research'}, {'name': u'Zacks Equity Research'}], 'summary': u"GoPro's (GPRO) Hero6 &amp; Fusion face formidable competition from lower-priced products. Let's discuss whether GoPro's products can withstand the competition and retain its market share.", 'content': [{'base': u'http://feed.zacks.com/commentary/AllStories/rss', 'type': u'text/html', 'value': u'<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>GoPro, Inc. </strong><a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/GPRO">GPRO</a> has been in the news again, thrust into the spotlight by the launch of the latest camera equipment from technology giant Alphabet Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/GOOGL">GOOGL</a>. The move was preceded by similar releases from other established tech companies, thus pitting GoPro&rsquo;s flagship cameras against tough competition, and forcing investors to question whether the Hero cameras can continue to hold their own in a rapidly expanding industry.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>The Evolution of Competition</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">In early days, GoPro had taken the action camera market by storm, but in recent times the company has grappled with stiff competition from lower-priced action camera alternatives.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Earlier this week, Google rolled out a camera called Google clips, which has a 12-megapixel sensor and a 130-degree field-of-view lens, with 8GB of internal memory. The camera is priced at just $249, which is half the cost of GoPro\'s new Hero6 camera. Even though Clips is not as advanced and high-tech as the Hero line-up, it is cheaper and comes from a well-known company. GoPro\'s market could suffer further as Alphabet leverages its brand value and channels to aggressively market this product.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Another such product is Sony Corporation&rsquo;s <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/SNE">SNE</a> latest action camera RX0 &mdash; which has features similar to GoPro&rsquo;s line, and is waterproof and shockproof as well. The RX0 is due to be released in October.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Then there is competition from Spectacles &mdash; Snap Inc.&rsquo;s <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/SNAP">SNAP</a> augmented reality and camera glasses &mdash; priced at $130. Olympus Tough TG &ndash;Tracker ($299), Garmin&rsquo;s VIRB Ultra 30 ($380) and VIRB XE ($310), Sony&rsquo;s FDR-X300 ($368), TomTom&rsquo;s Bandit Action Cam ($170) and Nikon&rsquo;s KeyMission 170 ($397) are a few of the other leading products which compete with the Hero cameras. GoPro&rsquo;s latest Hero6 camera is priced at $499.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Such lower-priced alternatives could corrode GoPro\'s market share and now, even its new video-editing software has a formidable competitor in Alphabet.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Amid an onslaught of such tough competition and with reviewers increasingly recommending cheaper alternatives, we believe GoPro\'s market share faces a very real threat. Granted, the company has a huge fan following, but it&rsquo;s increasingly plausible that its brand value might not be enough to fend off competition at this scale. Even its subscription and licensing revenue plans stand at risk, and might not be as successful as previously anticipated.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>GoPro&rsquo;s Kitty</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Late last month, GoPro unveiled the next version of its flagship action camera &mdash; the Hero6.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The latest Hero6 Black camera enables 4K video recording, with 60 fps, and 1080p recording, with 240fps. It boasts enhanced video stabilization, a built-in zoom that can be controlled from the touch screen, and packs 5Ghz for faster video offloads. The Hero6 Black operates on GoPro&rsquo;s new processor &mdash; GP1&mdash; and is quite a bit faster than its predecessor.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The company also launched Fusion, its new 5.2k 360-degree spherical camera designed to capture both virtual reality, and standard video and picture. Earlier there was Omni, a video rig with six cameras, but the Fusion looks to be a more user-friendly, affordable version for the masses.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Fusion&rsquo;s USP is something the company calls &ldquo;over-capture&rdquo; &mdash; which enables users to capture an entire scene, and then frame just the shots they want afterward in the GoPro app. &nbsp;Priced at $699, the camera&rsquo;s shipping commences in November.&nbsp;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">No doubt, Fusion will face tough competition from Garmin, VIRB 360 camera of which seems impressive, but costs a steep $800. There are several other spherical cameras already in the market. With GoPro\'s brand recognition and deep foothold in the action sports world, the company has a real chance to take the lead in this market, provided it gets Fusion right.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Getting it Right</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">GoPro has struggled in recent years, with messed-up product launches, operational stumbles and hitting the right price points. GoPro\'s shares have slumped nearly 70% in the last couple of years, as the company grappled with production delays and bungled up product roll outs, and lost ground to competitors like Sony, Garmin Ltd. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/GRMN">GRMN</a>, and Nikon Corporation <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/NINOY">NINOY</a>. This culminated in some significant layoffs, restructuring measures and the decision to shutter its nascent entertainment business.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">This year has been kinder to GoPro, as the company cut its losses and started to journey toward profitability. In fact, the company has been increasingly aligning itself with the smartphone era. Consider the content creation war between Facebook <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/FB">FB</a> and Snap &mdash; it shows a secular trend toward individualized, social content creation. GoPro&rsquo;s concept fits perfectly with this trend.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">However, the company&rsquo;s products have failed to achieve mass traction in the absence of an effective sharing aspect &mdash; which is a key element. Interestingly, GoPro is now working on making the smartphone the central focus of creating stories, which could help the company break out of its shell.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">To keep a hold of its fragile market share, GoPro has to make sure that it gets its products and pricing exactly right. We remain optimistic on the company&rsquo;s products, and hence have a Zacks Rank #2 (Buy) on GoPro. It comes in black and white colors and is priced at $399.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Pixelbook</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Pixelbook is a new 2-in-1, laptop-tablet hybrid from Google designed to compete with Microsoft <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/MSFT">MSFT</a> Surface. &nbsp;It has a 12.3-inch display, is super-thin with 10 mm thickness, weighs 2.2 pounds and comes with built in Google Assistant.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Its price starts at $999 and can go up to $1,649 for double the RAM, 512GB NVMe, and a seventh-generation Intel i7 processor. It supports a $99 pressure-sensitive stylus called Pixelbook Pen.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Google Clips </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It&rsquo;s a wireless camera that can connect to a phone and shoot photos and videos using AI. The device has a 130-degree field of view, 16 GB storage and doesn&rsquo;t need an Internet connection to function. It is priced at $249.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Pixel Buds </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">These are Google Assistant powered wireless headphones, the company&rsquo;s answer to Apple <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/AAPL">AAPL</a> AirPods. Priced at $160, it is available in the same colors as Pixel 2 and comes with a recharging pack and Google Translate built-in that can do real-time translation in 40 different languages.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Daydream View</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Next up is the latest Daydream View headset for $99 (previously $79). Things get a bit pricier around here for a wider field of view, face mask, color choices and a more immersive viewing experience.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is compatible with Pixel 2, LG V30, Samsung Galaxy S8 and Note 8.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>To Conclude </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">This is Google&rsquo;s second hardware event and just like last year, the company came up with some notable products and updates.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The tech giant&rsquo;s speed and scale of technological improvements clearly indicate that it refuses to rest on its past laurels and continues to adapt to changing market trends.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Alphabet carries a Zacks Rank #3 (Hold). u'http://www.zacks.com/stock/news/278016/targa-resources-trgp-inks-three-back-to-back-agreements?cid=CS-ZC-FT-278016', 'type': u'text/html', 'rel': u'alternate'}], 'title': u'Targa Resources (TRGP) Inks Three Back-to-Back Agreements', 'authors': [{'name': u'Zacks Equity Research'}, {'name': u'Zacks Equity Research'}], 'summary': u'Targa Resources (TRGP) consolidates its Permian Basin position through a clutch of deals.', 'content': [{'base': u'http://feed.zacks.com/commentary/AllStories/rss', 'type': u'text/html', 'value': u'<p style="text-align: justify;"><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml> <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>  <o:RelyOnVML></o:RelyOnVML>  <o:AllowPNG></o:AllowPNG> </o:OfficeDocumentSettings></xml><![endif]--></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Midstream service provider <b>Targa Resources Corp.</b> <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/TRGP">TRGP</a> recently announced the completion of the sale of 25% joint venture interest in the Grand Prix natural gas liquids (&quot;NGL&quot;) pipeline to private equity giant Blackstone Energy Partners. Simultaneously, Targa completed a deal with a portfolio company of Blackstone, EagleClaw Midstream Ventures, LLC. Also, Targa signed a letter of intent (&quot;LOI&quot;) with energy infrastructure provider Kinder Morgan <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/KMI">KMI</a> and DCP Midstream, LP <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/DCP">DCP</a> for jointly developing the proposed Gulf Coast Express Pipeline Project.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>Blackstone Deal</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">The Grand Prix pipeline will connect Permian Basin in west Texas and New Mexico to Targa&rsquo;s plant in Mont Belvieu, east of Houston. The pipeline will transport volumes from the Permian Basin and the company&rsquo;s North Texas system to its fractionation and storage complex in the NGL market hub at Mont Belvieu. Targa expects Grand Prix&rsquo;s transport capacity to be approximately 300,000 barrels per day (bpd), expandable up to 550,000 bpd. The pipeline is expected to come into service in the second quarter of 2019.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Targa expected the total capital expenditure associated with the Grand Prix project to be around $1.3 billion, out of which the company was supposed to spend approximately $250 million in 2017. The deal with Blackstone is expected to help Targa make ample net capital savings. It will also provide Targa financial and strategic benefits. Grand Prix is likely to enhance the company&rsquo;s ability to move customer volumes from the wellhead in the Permian Basin and North Texas to key petrochemical and export markets.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>EagleClaw Agreement</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">The EagleClaw deal supports a long-term Raw Product Purchase Agreement. Per the agreement, EagleClaw will receive transportation and fractionation services from Targa, as committed before, for the private natural gas gathering and processing company\'s Delaware Basin production. The deal is expected to provide Targa with long-term progressive fee-based cash flow.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>Gulf Coast Express Pipeline Project</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">The <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stock/news/277855/kinder-morgans-gcx-project-to-meet-permian-gas-demand">project</a> will serve the growing need for Permian Basin natural gas in the Texas Gulf Coast key markets. The pipeline will likely have the capacity to carry 1.92 billion cubic feet of natural gas every day, which is likely to commence operations by the second half of 2019. Kinder Morgan will construct and operate the pipeline project with a 50% stake. Targa Resources and DCP Midstream are each expected to have 25% ownership in the pipeline.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>About</b> <b>Targa Resources</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Headquartered in Houston, TX, Targa Resources Corp owns general and limited partner interests in Targa Resources Partners LP. It is engaged in providing midstream natural gas and natural gas liquid services in the United States. The company operates its business through two business segments: Natural Gas Gathering and Processing and NGL Logistics and Marketing. Targa also markets natural gas liquids produced and purchased in selected United States markets. The company also offers refinery services and wholesale propane marketing operations.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>Price Performance</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Targa Resources has lost 13.9% of its value year to date compared with the 6.2% fall of its <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/industry-rank/industry/oil-and-gas-refining-and-marketing-master-limited-partnerships-220">industry</a>.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><img alt="" src="https://staticx-tuner.zacks.com/images/zadmin_tuner_image/trgpkpd.jpg" /></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>Zacks Rank and Stock to Consider</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Targa Resources currently has a Zacks Rank #3 (Hold).</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">A better-ranked stock in the oil and energy sector is Lonestar Resources US Inc. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/LONE">LONE</a>. It sports a Zacks Rank #1 (Strong Buy). You can see <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/buy-list/?ADID=zp_1link&amp;ICID=zpi%20_1link"><b>the complete list of today&rsquo;s Zacks #1 Rank stocks here</b></a>.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Lonestar Resources&rsquo; sales for 2017 are expected to surge 60.2% year over year. The company delivered a positive earnings surprise of 62.5% in the second quarter of 2017.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><b>5 Trades Could Profit &quot;Big-League&quot; from Trump Policies</b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">If the stocks above spark your interest, wait until you look into companies primed to make substantial gains from Washington\'s changing course.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">Today Zacks reveals 5 tickers that could benefit from new trends like streamlined drug approvals, tariffs, lower taxes, higher interest rates, and spending surges in defense and infrastructure.</p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"><a 'content': [{'base': u'http://feed.zacks.com/commentary/AllStories/rss', 'type': u'text/html', 'value': u'<p style="text-align: justify;">The S&amp;P 500 breached a 20 year record on Thursday after hitting record close for six days on the trot. Also, the Dow and the Nasdaq notched up all-time highs. Meanwhile, the House of Representatives passed a $4.1 trillion budget bill for 2018. This package also includes $1.1 trillion for non-entitlement spending which further includes the U.S. defense budget for 2018.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The Dow Jones Industrial Average (DJIA) closed at 22,775.39, gaining 0.5%. The S&amp;P 500 Index (INX) increased 0.6% to close at 2,552.07. Meanwhile, the Nasdaq Composite Index (IXIC) closed at 6,585.36, increasing 0.8%. A total of 5.9 billion shares were traded on Thursday, lower than the last 20-session average of 6.2 billion shares. Advancing issues outnumbered decliners on the NYSE by 1.55-to-1 ratio. On the Nasdaq, advancers outnumbered decliners by 1.63-to-1 ratio. The CBOE VIX decreased 4.1% to close at 9.24.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Benchmarks Break New Boundaries</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">The S&amp;P 500 garnered 14.33 points on Thursday to mark its sixth consecutive record close &mdash; its longest run of record closes since 1997. With this, the S&amp;P 500 registered its 43rd record for 2017. Moreover, the S&amp;P 500 has ended in the positive for the past eight successive sessions, the longest since 2013. Of the 11 major sectors of the S&amp;P 500, 10 ended in the green, with financials and technology leading the advancers. The Technology Select Sector SPDR ETF (XLK) and Financial Select Sector SPDR ETF (XLF) both gained 1%.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The Dow amassed almost 114 points to notch up all-time intraday and closing records. This also registered its 46th record for 2017. Such gains were made possible by a surge in shares of Goldman Sachs <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/GS">GS</a> and Boeing <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/BA">BA</a>, which gained 2.4% and 1.2%, respectively. Both the companies possess a Zacks Rank #3 (Hold). You can see <a href="https://www.zacks.com/stocks/buy-list/?ADID=zp_1link&amp;ICID=zpi%20_1link">the complete list of today&rsquo;s Zacks #1 Rank (Strong Buy) stocks here</a>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The Nasdaq clinched intraday and closing records as well after advancing almost 51 points. Meanwhile, the Russell 2000 index added 4.32 points to increase 0.3% and closed at 1,512.09 &mdash; coming within a fraction of its record close.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>House Passes the Budget Bill</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">In its first definitive move toward tax reforms, the House of Representatives passed $4.1 trillion 2018 budget legislation on Thursday. This boosted investors&rsquo; sentiment and the economists expect this to be signed into law by the year end. The Republicans voted 219 to 206 in favor of the amendment. However, a few from President Trump&rsquo;s team voted against the bill along with Democrats, objecting to parts of the tax reform proposal. The Democrats, meanwhile, opposed passing of the bill, terming the move as &quot;a vehicle for achieving partisan tax reform.&quot;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Terms of the budget bill state that around $1.1 trillion would be allocated for non-entitlement spending which would include a defense budget of $622 billion. Passing of the budget resolution is particularly important for the Republicans as this would ultimately culminate into a process known as reconciliation. This would help the members of GOP to pass the tax reform bill in the Senate with just 51 votes as majority instead of the normally followed 60-votes rule.&nbsp; Moreover, the Senate Budget Committee was slated to pass a budget bill similar to the one passed by the House.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">As the Republicans remain divided over the amount by which tax rates will be slashed, analysts feel that it would not be an easy task for the GOP to through such reforms. The markets, however, have gained traction since the new tax code was introduced by the Trump administration.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Economic Data</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">The initial claims decreased to 260,000 from 272,000 in the previous week. This also came in below the consensus estimate of 266,000. Meanwhile, the trade balance decreased to $42.4 billion and came in below the consensus estimate of a decrease to $42.9 billion. margin is the most important entry in an income statement as it demonstrates the affluence of a company. It determines the efficiency of a company in deploying its resources, making it the most suitable metric for the measurement of a company&rsquo;s profitability. &nbsp;<br /><br /><strong>Net Profit Margin</strong> = <strong>Net profit </strong>/<strong>Sales</strong> * 100.<br /><br />In simple terms, net profit is the amount a company retains after deducting all costs, interest, depreciation, taxes and other expenses. In fact, net profit margin can turn out to be a potent point of reference to gauge the strength in a company&rsquo;s operations and cost-control measures.<br /><br />Higher net profit is essential for rewarding stakeholders. Net margin helps investors judge the risks of investing in a company. Creditors also view it as a major factor in determining a company&rsquo;s ability to pay off debts.<br /><br />Moreover, a higher net profit margin as compared to peers lends a competitive edge. Strength in the metric not only attracts investors but also draws well-skilled employees that eventually add to the value of the business.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Pros and Cons</strong><br /><br />Net profit margin helps investors gain clarity on a company&rsquo;s business model in terms of pricing policy, cost structure and manufacturing efficiency. Hence, a strong net profit margin is preferred by all classes of investors.<br /><br />However, net profit margin as an investment criterion has its own share of pitfalls. The metric varies widely from industry to industry. While net income is a key metric for investment measurement in traditional industries, it is not that important for technology companies.<br /><br />Moreover, the difference in accounting treatment of various items &mdash; especially non-cash expenses like depreciation and stock-based compensation &mdash; makes comparison a daunting task.<br /><br />Further, for companies preferring to grow with debt, instead of equity funding, higher interest expenses usually weigh on the net profit. In such cases, the measure is rendered ineffective to analyze a company&rsquo;s performance.<br /><br /><strong>The Winning Strategy</strong><br /><br />A healthy net profit margin and solid EPS growth are the two most sought-after elements in a business model.<br /><br />Apart from these, we have added a few other criteria to ensure maximum returns from this strategy.<br /><br /><strong>Screening Parameters</strong><br /><br /><strong>Net Margin 12 months &ndash; Most Recent (%) greater than equal to 0</strong>: High net profit margin indicates solid profitability.<br /><br /><strong>Percentage Change in EPS F(0)/(F-1) greater than equal to 0</strong>: It indicates earnings growth.<br /><br /><strong>Average Broker Rating (1-5) equal to 1</strong>: A rating of #1 indicates brokers&rsquo; extreme bullishness of the stock.<br /><br /><strong>Zacks Rank less than or equal to 2</strong>: Stocks having a Zacks Rank #1 (Strong Buy) or 2 (Buy) generally perform better than their peers in all types of market environment.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.zacks.com/style-scores-education/"><strong>VGM Score</strong></a> of A or B: Our research shows that stocks with a VGM Score of A or B when combined with a Zacks Rank #1 or 2 offer the best upside potential.<br /><br />Here are five of the 17 stocks that qualified the screen:<br /><br /><strong>Johnson Outdoors Inc</strong>. <a href="http://www.zacks.com/stock/quote/JOUT">JOUT</a> is a leading global outdoor recreation company that designs, manufactures and markets a portfolio of winning, consumer-preferred brands across four categories: Watercraft, Marine Electronics, Diving and Outdoor Equipment.
